[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to calculate the probability of each possible outcome and then find the weighted average of these outcomes. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 1: Calculate the probability of selecting a black ball from bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin A contains 1 white ball and 4 black balls. The total number of balls in bin A is \(1 + 4 = 5\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a black ball from bin A is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{Black from A}) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 2: Calculate the probability of selecting a white ball from bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a white ball from bin A is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{White from A}) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 3: Calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin B given that a black ball was selected from bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m If a black ball is selected from bin A, a ball is randomly selected from bin B. Bin B contains 3 balls labeled \(\$1\) and 1 ball labeled \(\$7\). The total number of balls in bin B is \(3 + 1 = 4\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$1\) from bin B is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\$1 \text{ from B} \mid \text{Black from A}) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$7\) from bin B is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\$7 \text{ from B} \mid \text{Black from A}) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 4: Calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin W given that a white ball was selected from bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m If a white ball is selected from bin A, a ball is randomly selected from bin W. Bin W contains 5 balls labeled \(\$8\) and 1 ball labeled \(\$500\). The total number of balls in bin W is \(5 + 1 = 6\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$8\) from bin W is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\$8 \text{ from W} \mid \text{White from A}) = \frac{5}{6}

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$500\) from bin W is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\$500 \text{ from W} \mid \text{White from A}) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 5: Calculate the overall probability of each outcome
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m We need to find the overall probability of each possible outcome by combining the probabilities from steps 3 and 4 with the probabilities from step 1.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Outcome 1: Black from A and \$1 from B
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{Black from A} \cap \$1 \text{ from B}) = P(\text{Black from A}) \times P(\$1 \text{ from B} \mid \text{Black from A}) = \frac{4}{5} \times \frac{3}{4} = \frac{3}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Outcome 2: Black from A and \$7 from B
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{Black from A} \cap \$7 \text{ from B}) = P(\text{Black from A}) \times P(\$7 \text{ from B} \mid \text{Black from A}) = \frac{4}{5} \times \frac{1}{4} = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Outcome 3: White from A and \$8 from W
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Outcome 4: White from A and \$500 from W

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 6: Calculate the expected win

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \frac{3}{5} = \frac{3 \times 6}{5 \times 6} = \frac{18}{30}

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities of selecting each type of ball from each bin and the corresponding winnings. Let's break down the problem step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 1: Determine the probabilities of selecting each type of ball from each bin
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 1. **Bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a white ball: \(\frac{1}{5}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a black ball: \(\frac{4}{5}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 2. **Bin B:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$1\): \(\frac{3}{4}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$7\): \(\frac{1}{4}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 3. **Bin W:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$8\): \(\frac{5}{6}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$500\): \(\frac{1}{6}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 2: Calculate the expected winnings for each scenario
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Scenario 1: Selecting a white ball from Bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - Probability of selecting a white ball from Bin A: \(\frac{1}{5}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - If a white ball is selected, a ball is randomly selected from Bin W.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m   - Expected winnings from Bin W: \(\frac{1}{2} \times \$8 + \frac{1}{2} \times \$500 = \$4 + \$250 = \$254\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - Expected winnings for this scenario: \(\frac{1}{5} \times \$254 = \$50.80\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Scenario 2: Selecting a black ball from Bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - Probability of selecting a black ball from Bin A: \(\frac{4}{5}\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - If a black ball is selected, a ball is randomly selected from Bin B.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m   - Expected winnings from Bin B: \(\frac{1}{2} \times \$1 + \frac{1}{2} \times \$7 = \$0.50 + \$3.50 = \$4\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - Expected winnings for this scenario: \(\frac{4}{5} \times \$4 = \$3.20\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 3: Combine the expected winnings from both scenarios
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m

You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities of selecting each ball from each bin and the corresponding winnings. Let's break down the problem step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 1: Determine the probabilities of selecting each ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin \(A\) contains 1 white ball and 4 black balls. The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 2: Determine the probabilities of selecting each ball from bin \(B\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin \(B\) contains 3 balls labeled \(\$1\) and 1 ball labeled \(\$7\). The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$1\) from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{\$1 from } B) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$7\) from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{\$7 from } B) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 3: Determine the probabilities of selecting each ball from bin \(W\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin \(W\) contains 5 balls labeled \(\$8\) and 1 ball labeled \(\$500\). The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$8\) from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{\$8 from } W) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$500\) from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{\$500 from } W) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 4: Calculate the expected winnings
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m We need to consider the expected winnings based on the outcomes of the first draw from bin \(A\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 1. **If a white ball is selected from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The probability of this happening is \(P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$8\) from bin \(W\) is \(P(\text{\$8 from } W) = \frac{5}{6}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$500\) from bin \(W\) is \(P(\text{\$500 from } W) = \frac{1}{6}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The expected winnings in this case is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      \left(\frac{5}{6} \times 8\right) + \left(\frac{1}{6} \times 500\right) = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = 90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 2. **If a black ball is selected from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The probability of this happening is \(P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$1\) from bin \(B\) is \(P(\text{\$1 from } B) = \frac{3}{4}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$7\) from bin \(B\) is \(P(\text{\$7 from } B) = \frac{1}{4}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - The expected winnings in this case is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      \left(\frac{3}{4} \times 1\right) + \left(\frac{1}{4} \times 7\right) = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \frac{10}{4} = 2.5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 5: Combine the expected winnings

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities of selecting each ball from each bin and the corresponding winnings. Let's break down the problem step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 1: Determine the probabilities of selecting each ball from each bin
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 1. **Bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a white ball: \( P(W_A) = \frac{1}{5} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a black ball: \( P(B_A) = \frac{4}{5} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 2. **Bin B:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting the \$1 ball: \( P(1_B) = \frac{3}{4} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting the \$7 ball: \( P(7_B) = \frac{1}{4} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 3. **Bin W:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting the \$8 ball: \( P(8_W) = \frac{5}{6} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting the \$500 ball: \( P(500_W) = \frac{1}{6} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 2: Calculate the expected winnings
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m We need to consider the expected winnings for each possible outcome of the first draw from Bin A and then the second draw from the selected bin.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Case 1: Selecting a white ball from Bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - Probability: \( P(W_A) = \frac{1}{5} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - If a white ball is selected, a ball is drawn from Bin W.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m   - Expected winnings from Bin W: \( E(W_W) = \left( \frac{5}{6} \times 8 \right) + \left( \frac{1}{6} \times 500 \right) = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = 90 \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m #### Case 2: Selecting a black ball from Bin A
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - Probability: \( P(B_A) = \frac{4}{5} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m - If a black ball is selected, a ball is drawn from Bin B.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m   - Expected winnings from Bin B: \( E(B_B) = \left( \frac{3}{4} \times 1 \right) + \left( \frac{1}{4} \times 7 \right) = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \frac{10}{4} = 2.5 \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 3: Combine the expected winnings

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$. You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to calculate the expected value of the winnings. We will do this by considering the probabilities of each possible outcome and the corresponding winnings.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 1: Determine the probabilities and winnings for each scenario
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 1. **Scenario 1: Selecting a black ball from bin \( A \)**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \): \( P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), a ball is randomly selected from bin \( B \).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$1\) from bin \( B \): \( P(\$1 \text{ from } B) = \frac{3}{4} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$7\) from bin \( B \): \( P(\$7 \text{ from } B) = \frac{1}{4} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Expected winnings from this scenario: \( E_1 = \left(\frac{3}{4} \times 1\right) + \left(\frac{1}{4} \times 7\right) = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \frac{10}{4} = 2.5 \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 2. **Scenario 2: Selecting a white ball from bin \( A \)**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \): \( P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - If a white ball is selected from bin \( A \), a ball is randomly selected from bin \( W \).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$8\) from bin \( W \): \( P(\$8 \text{ from } W) = \frac{5}{6} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m      - Probability of selecting a ball labeled \(\$500\) from bin \( W \): \( P(\$500 \text{ from } W) = \frac{1}{6} \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m    - Expected winnings from this scenario: \( E_2 = \left(\frac{5}{6} \times 8\right) + \left(\frac{1}{6} \times 500\right) = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = 90 \)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 2: Calculate the overall expected winnings
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The overall expected winnings \( E \) is the weighted average of the expected winnings from each scenario, weighted by their respective probabilities:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E = P(\text{Black from } A) \times E_1 + P(\text{White from } A) \times E_2
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E = \left(\frac{4}{5}\right) \times 2.5 + \left(\frac{1}{5}\right) \times 90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E = \frac{4 \times 2.5}{5} + \frac{90}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E = \frac{10}{5} + \frac{90}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E = 2 + 18
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E = 20
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [prompt] system
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to calculate the expected value of the amount won based on the outcomes of the two draws. Let's break down the problem step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 1: Calculate the probability of drawing a black ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Bin \(A\) contains 1 white ball and 4 black balls. The probability of drawing a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 2: Calculate the probability of drawing a white ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The probability of drawing a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 3: Calculate the expected value of the amount won if a black ball is drawn from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m If a black ball is drawn from bin \(A\), a ball is then drawn from bin \(B\). Bin \(B\) contains 3 balls labeled \(\$1\) and 1 ball labeled \(\$7\). The probability of drawing each ball from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\$1 \text{ from } B) = \frac{3}{4}, \quad P(\$7 \text{ from } B) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The expected value of the amount won if a black ball is drawn from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E(\text{Win} \mid \text{Black from } A) = \left(\frac{3}{4} \times 1\right) + \left(\frac{1}{4} \times 7\right) = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \frac{10}{4} = 2.5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 4: Calculate the expected value of the amount won if a white ball is drawn from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m If a white ball is drawn from bin \(A\), a ball is then drawn from bin \(W\). Bin \(W\) contains 5 balls labeled \(\$8\) and 1 ball labeled \(\$500\). The probability of drawing each ball from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m P(\$8 \text{ from } W) = \frac{5}{6}, \quad P(\$500 \text{ from } W) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The expected value of the amount won if a white ball is drawn from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E(\text{Win} \mid \text{White from } A) = \left(\frac{5}{6} \times 8\right) + \left(\frac{1}{6} \times 500\right) = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = 90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m ### Step 5: Calculate the overall expected value of the amount won
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m The overall expected value of the amount won is the weighted average of the expected values from the two scenarios, weighted by the probabilities of each scenario:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E(\text{Win}) = P(\text{Black from } A) \times E(\text{Win} \mid \text{Black from } A) + P(\text{White from } A) \times E(\text{Win} \mid \text{White from } A)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Substituting the values we calculated:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m E(\text{Win}) = \left(\frac{4}{5} \times 2.5\right) + \left(\frac{1}{5} \times 90\right) = \frac{10}{5} + \frac{90}{5} = 2 + 18 = 20
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m Thus, the expected win is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \boxed{20}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2561063)[0m \]
